    Dear Colleagues, As a follow-up to UNRWAâ€™s decision of last month regarding the payment modalities for daily paid workers, I am pleased to announce that the Commissioner-General has decided to extend the same modalities for the month of May, namely that:



    1. All daily paid workers who were authorized to work in May, whether they did so in person on UNRWA premises or remotely, will be paid in full as stipulated in their contract;



    2. All daily paid workers who were not able to perform the tasks stipulated in their contracts will receive 50% of the payments expected for the months of May, despite the suspension of their duties.



    Please note that every field will apply its own end-of-school date to the modalities applicable to school workers.



    We take this opportunity to wish the UNRWA family a blessed Eid al-Fitr.



    Kind regards,



    Antonino



    Antonino BrusÃ¡ (Mr.) | Director of Human Resources
